    WHEN [a0].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN COALESCE([a0].[HouseNumber], N'') + N',' + COALESCE([a0].[StreetName], N'') + N',' + COALESCE([a0].[Ward], N'') + N',' + COALESCE([a0].[District], N'') + N',' + COALESCE([a0].[Country], N'')
END AS [AddressThuongTru], CASE
    WHEN [a1].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN COALESCE([a1].[HouseNumber], N'') + N',' + COALESCE([a1].[StreetName], N'') + N',' + COALESCE([a1].[Ward], N'') + N',' + COALESCE([a1].[District], N'') + N',' + COALESCE([a1].[Country], N'')
END AS [AddressTamTru], [s].[Email], [s].[SoDienThoai], [s].[QuocTich], [s2].[Name] AS [Status]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [Departments] AS [d] ON [s].[DepartmentId] = [d].[Id]
INNER JOIN [SchoolYears] AS [s0] ON [s].[SchoolYearId] = [s0].[Id]
INNER JOIN [StudyPrograms] AS [s1] ON [s].[StudyProgramId] = [s1].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Addresses] AS [a] ON [s].[DiaChiNhanThuId] = [a].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [Addresses] AS [a0] ON [s].[DiaChiThuongTruId] = [a0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [Addresses] AS [a1] ON [s].[DiaChiTamTruId] = [a1].[Id]
INNER JOIN [StudentStatuses] AS [s2] ON [s].[StatusId] = [s2].[Id]
